{'role': 'assistant', 'content': '## Fixed! üéØ\n\nI found and fixed the critical bug that was preventing PT051 training records and NEO Build from working!\n\n### The Root Cause\n\nThe `/api/scores` endpoint returns:\n```json\n{\n  "scores": [["Anderson, Benjamin ‚Äì ADF305", [{...scores...}]], ...],\n  "count": 1612\n}\n```\n\nBut `fetchScores()` was trying to parse it as:\n```typescript\nconst result = await fetchAPI<Record<string, Score[]>>(url);\nreturn new Map(Object.entries(result.data));\n```\n\nThis was treating `result.data` as `{ "traineeName": [...] }` instead of the actual structure `{ scores: [[...]], count: ... }`.\n\n**Result:** `result.data` was the entire response object, not just the scores array, so the Map conversion was creating an empty Map!\n\n### The Fix\n\nUpdated `fetchScores()` to correctly access the scores array:\n```typescript\nconst result = await fetchAPI<{ scores: [string, Score[]][], count: number }>(url);\nif (result.success && result.data && result.data.scores) {\n  // Convert [[traineeName, [scoreObjects]]] to Map<string, Score[]>\n  return new Map(result.data.scores);\n}\n```\n\n### What This Fixes\n\n1. ‚úÖ **PT051 Training Records** - Will now show LMP scores in HateSheetView\n2. ‚úÖ **NEO Build** - Will now use actual trainee progress data from database to schedule flights\n3. ‚úÖ **Score Data Loading** - All 1,612 scores for 112 trainees will now be available\n\n### Deployment\n\n**Commit:** `c38ad5e` - "Fix scores API response parsing and add debug logging"\n**Status:** Pushed to GitHub, Railway deploying now (2-5 minutes)\n\n### Testing\n\nAfter Railway deployment completes:\n1.
